\hypertarget{_dlgcode_8c}{}\section{Common/\+Dlgcode.c File Reference}
\label{_dlgcode_8c}\index{Common/\+Dlgcode.\+c@{Common/\+Dlgcode.\+c}}


Function that manage warning and error dialog proc, threads, help balloon interactions, drivers, file system... Some functions are used to work on volumes and partitions. There is also some functions to launch a benchmark.

H\+DC \hyperlink{_dlgcode_8c_a27c6044a8e5fb39c2d40031a9d09a2f9}{Create\+Mem\+Bitmap} (H\+I\+N\+S\+T\+A\+N\+CE h\+Instance, H\+W\+ND hwnd, char $\ast$resource)

H\+B\+I\+T\+M\+AP \hyperlink{_dlgcode_8c_a6d6a25e4338d75cb5d87bcc297d1ca03}{Render\+Bitmap} (char $\ast$resource, H\+W\+ND hwnd\+Dest, int x, int y, int n\+Width, int n\+Height, B\+O\+OL b\+Direct\+Render, B\+O\+OL b\+Keep\+Aspect\+Ratio)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Renders the specified bitmap at the specified location and stretches it to fit (anti-\/aliasing is applied). If b\+Direct\+Render is F\+A\+L\+SE and both n\+Width and n\+Height are zero, the width and height of hwnd\+Dest are retrieved and adjusted according to screen D\+PI (the width and height of the resultant image are adjusted the same way); furthermore, if b\+Keep\+Aspect\+Ratio is T\+R\+UE, the smaller D\+PI factor of the two (i.\+e. horiz. or vert.) is used both for horiz. and vert. scaling (note that the overall G\+UI aspect ratio changes irregularly in both directions depending on the D\+PI). If b\+Direct\+Render is T\+R\+UE, b\+Keep\+Aspect\+Ratio is ignored. This function returns a handle to the scaled bitmap. When the bitmap is no longer needed, it should be deleted by calling Delete\+Object() with the handle passed as the parameter. Known Windows issues\+: \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

B\+O\+OL \hyperlink{_dlgcode_8c_af5112411ed301354da0bb9373d1b5f6f}{Get\+Sys\+Device\+Paths} (H\+W\+ND hwnd\+Dlg)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Stores the device path of the system partition in Sys\+Partition\+Device\+Path and the device path of the system drive in Sys\+Drive\+Device\+Path. I\+M\+P\+O\+R\+T\+A\+NT\+: As this may take a very long time if called for the first time, it should be called only before performing a dangerous operation (such as header backup restore or formatting a supposedly non-\/system device) never at W\+M\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+D\+I\+A\+L\+OG or any other G\+UI events -- instead call Is\+System\+Device\+Path (path, hwnd\+Dlg, F\+A\+L\+SE) for very fast preliminary G\+UI checks; also note that right after the \char`\"{}\+Select Device\char`\"{} dialog exits with an OK return code, you can use the global flags b\+Sys\+Partition\+Selected and b\+Sys\+Drive\+Selected to see if the user selected the system partition/device. After this function completes successfully, the results are cached for the rest of the session and repeated executions complete very fast. Returns T\+R\+UE if successful (otherwise F\+A\+L\+SE). \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
int \hyperlink{_dlgcode_8c_a83d99c4efd2e6e3f507dd7da5a8b4280}{Is\+System\+Device\+Path} (char $\ast$path, H\+W\+ND hwnd\+Dlg, B\+O\+OL b\+Reliable\+Required)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Determines whether the device path is the path of the system partition or of the system drive (or neither). If b\+Reliable\+Required is T\+R\+UE, very fast execution is guaranteed, but the results cannot be relied upon. If it\textquotesingle{}s F\+A\+L\+SE and the function is called for the first time, execution may take up to one minute but the results are reliable. I\+M\+P\+O\+R\+T\+A\+NT\+: As the execution may take a very long time if called for the first time with b\+Reliable\+Required set to T\+R\+UE, it should be called with b\+Reliable\+Required set to T\+R\+UE only before performing a dangerous operation (such as header backup restore or formatting a supposedly non-\/system device) never at W\+M\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+D\+I\+A\+L\+OG or any other G\+UI events (use Is\+System\+Device\+Path(path, hwnd\+Dlg, F\+A\+L\+S\+E) for fast preliminary G\+UI checks; also note that right after the \char`\"{}\+Select Device\char`\"{} dialog exits with an OK return code, you can use the global flags b\+Sys\+Partition\+Selected and b\+Sys\+Drive\+Selected to see if the user selected the system partition/device). After this function completes successfully, the results are cached for the rest of the session, b\+Reliable\+Required is ignored (T\+R\+UE implied), repeated executions complete very fast, and the results are always reliable. Return codes\+: 1 -\/ it is the system partition path (e.\+g. ) 2 -\/ it is the system drive path (e.\+g. ) 3 -\/ it is the extra boot partition path 0 -\/ it\textquotesingle{}s not the system partition/drive path -\/1 -\/ the result can\textquotesingle{}t be determined, isn\textquotesingle{}t reliable, or there was an error. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em The function accepts two input formats\+: Input format 1\+: \{0, \char`\"{}\+M\+E\+S\+S\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+I\+D\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+B\+U\+T\+T\+O\+N\+\_\+1\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+I\+D\char`\"{}, ... \char`\"{}\+L\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+B\+U\+T\+T\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+I\+D\char`\"{}, 0\}; Input format 2\+: \{L\char`\"{}\char`\"{}, L\char`\"{}\+Message text\char`\"{}, L\char`\"{}\+Button caption 1\char`\"{}, ... L\char`\"{}\+Last button caption\char`\"{}, 0\}; The second format is to be used if any of the strings contains format specification (e.\+g. s, d) or in any other cases where a string needs to be resolved before calling this function. If the returned value is 0, the user closed the dialog window without making a choice. If the user made a choice, the returned value is the ordinal number of the choice (1..M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+O\+I\+C\+ES) \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Check if the os version is a least over the first supported version Returns T\+R\+UE if the operating system is at least req\+Min\+OS and service pack at least req\+Min\+Service\+Pack. Example 1\+: Is\+O\+S\+Version\+At\+Least (W\+I\+N\+\_\+\+V\+I\+S\+TA, 1) called under Windows 2008, returns T\+R\+UE. Example 2\+: Is\+O\+S\+Version\+At\+Least (W\+I\+N\+\_\+\+XP, 3) called under Windows XP S\+P1, returns F\+A\+L\+SE. \subsection{Detailed Description}
Function that manage warning and error dialog proc, threads, help balloon interactions, drivers, file system... Some functions are used to work on volumes and partitions. There is also some functions to launch a benchmark. 

\begin{DoxyVersion}{Version}
1.\+3.\+1 
\end{DoxyVersion}
\begin{DoxyDate}{Date}
20/01/2017 
\end{DoxyDate}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Accommodate\+Text\+Field()}{AccommodateTextField()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Accommodate\+Text\+Field (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{H\+W\+ND}]{hwnd\+Dlg,  }\item[{U\+I\+NT}]{ctrl\+Id,  }\item[{B\+O\+OL}]{b\+First\+Update,  }\item[{H\+F\+O\+NT}]{h\+Font }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Resizes a text field according to its actual width and height in pixels (font size is taken into account) and moves it accordingly if the field is centered or right-\/aligned. Should be used on all hyperlinks upon dialog init after localization (b\+First\+Update should be T\+R\+UE) and later whenever a hyperlink text changes (b\+First\+Update must be F\+A\+L\+SE).

\index{Dlgcode.\+c@{Dlgcode.\+c}!Ask\+Multi\+Choice@{Ask\+Multi\+Choice}}
\index{Ask\+Multi\+Choice@{Ask\+Multi\+Choice}!Dlgcode.\+c@{Dlgcode.\+c}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Ask\+Multi\+Choice()}{AskMultiChoice()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int Ask\+Multi\+Choice (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void $\ast$}]{strings\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Bold }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



The function accepts two input formats\+: Input format 1\+: \{0, \char`\"{}\+M\+E\+S\+S\+A\+G\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+I\+D\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+B\+U\+T\+T\+O\+N\+\_\+1\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+I\+D\char`\"{}, ... \char`\"{}\+L\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+B\+U\+T\+T\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+I\+D\char`\"{}, 0\}; Input format 2\+: \{L\char`\"{}\char`\"{}, L\char`\"{}\+Message text\char`\"{}, L\char`\"{}\+Button caption 1\char`\"{}, ... L\char`\"{}\+Last button caption\char`\"{}, 0\}; The second format is to be used if any of the strings contains format specification (e.\+g. s, d) or in any other cases where a string needs to be resolved before calling this function. If the returned value is 0, the user closed the dialog window without making a choice. If the user made a choice, the returned value is the ordinal number of the choice (1..M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+O\+I\+C\+ES) 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em B\+O\+OL} & b\+Bold \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em void} & $\ast$ strings\mbox{[}\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

int Dialog\+Box\+ParamW (h\+Inst, M\+A\+K\+E\+I\+N\+T\+R\+E\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+EW (I\+D\+D\+\_\+\+M\+U\+L\+T\+I\+\_\+\+C\+H\+O\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+D\+LG), Main\+Dlg, (D\+L\+G\+P\+R\+OC) Multi\+Choice\+Dialog\+Proc, (L\+P\+A\+R\+AM) \&params)

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Auxiliary\+Dlg\+Proc()}{AuxiliaryDlgProc()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily B\+O\+OL C\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+CK Auxiliary\+Dlg\+Proc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{H\+W\+ND}]{hwnd\+Dlg,  }\item[{U\+I\+NT}]{msg,  }\item[{W\+P\+A\+R\+AM}]{w\+Param,  }\item[{L\+P\+A\+R\+AM}]{l\+Param }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This function currently serves the following purposes\+: 


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Determines scaling factors for current screen D\+PI and G\+UI aspect ratio.
\item Determines how Windows skews the G\+UI aspect ratio (which happens when the user has a non-\/default D\+PI). The determined values must be used when performing some G\+UI operations and calculations.

\end{DoxyReturn}

Returns the free space on the specified partition (volume) in bytes. If the \textquotesingle{}occupied\+Bytes\textquotesingle{} pointer is not N\+U\+LL, size of occupied space (in bytes) is written to the pointed location. In addition, if the \textquotesingle{}percent\textquotesingle{} pointer is not N\+U\+LL, \% of free space is stored in the pointed location. If there\textquotesingle{}s an error, returns -\/1.

\index{Dlgcode.\+c@{Dlgcode.\+c}!Get\+Sys\+Device\+Paths@{Get\+Sys\+Device\+Paths}}
\index{Get\+Sys\+Device\+Paths@{Get\+Sys\+Device\+Paths}!Dlgcode.\+c@{Dlgcode.\+c}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Get\+Sys\+Device\+Paths()}{GetSysDevicePaths()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily B\+O\+OL Get\+Sys\+Device\+Paths (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{H\+W\+ND}]{hwnd\+Dlg }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Stores the device path of the system partition in Sys\+Partition\+Device\+Path and the device path of the system drive in Sys\+Drive\+Device\+Path. I\+M\+P\+O\+R\+T\+A\+NT\+: As this may take a very long time if called for the first time, it should be called only before performing a dangerous operation (such as header backup restore or formatting a supposedly non-\/system device) never at W\+M\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+D\+I\+A\+L\+OG or any other G\+UI events -- instead call Is\+System\+Device\+Path (path, hwnd\+Dlg, F\+A\+L\+SE) for very fast preliminary G\+UI checks; also note that right after the \char`\"{}\+Select Device\char`\"{} dialog exits with an OK return code, you can use the global flags b\+Sys\+Partition\+Selected and b\+Sys\+Drive\+Selected to see if the user selected the system partition/device. After this function completes successfully, the results are cached for the rest of the session and repeated executions complete very fast. Returns T\+R\+UE if successful (otherwise F\+A\+L\+SE). 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em H\+W\+ND} & hwnd\+Dlg \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
B\+O\+OL (b\+Cached\+Sys\+Device\+Paths\+Valid \&\& strlen (Sys\+Partition\+Device\+Path) $>$ 1 \&\& strlen (Sys\+Drive\+Device\+Path) $>$ 1) 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{_dlgcode_8c_a920ebed5095721b60d2fc255ac9a1437}\label{_dlgcode_8c_a920ebed5095721b60d2fc255ac9a1437}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Is\+O\+S\+Version\+At\+Least()}{IsOSVersionAtLeast()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily B\+O\+OL Is\+O\+S\+Version\+At\+Least (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{O\+S\+Version\+Enum}]{req\+Min\+OS,  }\item[{int}]{req\+Min\+Service\+Pack }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Check if the os version is a least over the first supported version Returns T\+R\+UE if the operating system is at least req\+Min\+OS and service pack at least req\+Min\+Service\+Pack. Example 1\+: Is\+O\+S\+Version\+At\+Least (W\+I\+N\+\_\+\+V\+I\+S\+TA, 1) called under Windows 2008, returns T\+R\+UE. Example 2\+: Is\+O\+S\+Version\+At\+Least (W\+I\+N\+\_\+\+XP, 3) called under Windows XP S\+P1, returns F\+A\+L\+SE. Example 3\+: Is\+O\+S\+Version\+At\+Least (W\+I\+N\+\_\+\+XP, 3) called under Windows Vista S\+P1, returns T\+R\+UE.

\index{Dlgcode.\+c@{Dlgcode.\+c}!Is\+System\+Device\+Path@{Is\+System\+Device\+Path}}
\index{Is\+System\+Device\+Path@{Is\+System\+Device\+Path}!Dlgcode.\+c@{Dlgcode.\+c}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Is\+System\+Device\+Path()}{IsSystemDevicePath()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int Is\+System\+Device\+Path (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char $\ast$}]{path,  }\item[{H\+W\+ND}]{hwnd\+Dlg,  }\item[{B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Reliable\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Determines whether the device path is the path of the system partition or of the system drive (or neither). If b\+Reliable\+Required is T\+R\+UE, very fast execution is guaranteed, but the results cannot be relied upon. If it\textquotesingle{}s F\+A\+L\+SE and the function is called for the first time, execution may take up to one minute but the results are reliable. I\+M\+P\+O\+R\+T\+A\+NT\+: As the execution may take a very long time if called for the first time with b\+Reliable\+Required set to T\+R\+UE, it should be called with b\+Reliable\+Required set to T\+R\+UE only before performing a dangerous operation (such as header backup restore or formatting a supposedly non-\/system device) never at W\+M\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+D\+I\+A\+L\+OG or any other G\+UI events (use Is\+System\+Device\+Path(path, hwnd\+Dlg, F\+A\+L\+S\+E) for fast preliminary G\+UI checks; also note that right after the \char`\"{}\+Select Device\char`\"{} dialog exits with an OK return code, you can use the global flags b\+Sys\+Partition\+Selected and b\+Sys\+Drive\+Selected to see if the user selected the system partition/device). After this function completes successfully, the results are cached for the rest of the session, b\+Reliable\+Required is ignored (T\+R\+UE implied), repeated executions complete very fast, and the results are always reliable. Return codes\+: 1 -\/ it is the system partition path (e.\+g. ) 2 -\/ it is the system drive path (e.\+g. ) 3 -\/ it is the extra boot partition path 0 -\/ it\textquotesingle{}s not the system partition/drive path -\/1 -\/ the result can\textquotesingle{}t be determined, isn\textquotesingle{}t reliable, or there was an error. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em B\+O\+OL} & b\+Reliable\+Required \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em H\+W\+ND} & hwnd\+Dlg \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em char} & $\ast$ path \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
int -\/1 if (!b\+Cached\+Sys\+Device\+Paths\+Valid \&\& b\+Reliable\+Required \&\& !\+Get\+Sys\+Device\+Paths (hwnd\+Dlg)) -\/1 if (strlen (Sys\+Partition\+Device\+Path) $<$= 1 $\vert$$\vert$ strlen (Sys\+Drive\+Device\+Path) $<$= 1) 1 if (strncmp (path, Sys\+Partition\+Device\+Path, max (strlen(path), strlen(\+Sys\+Partition\+Device\+Path))) == 0) 2 else if (strncmp (path, Sys\+Drive\+Device\+Path, max (strlen(path), strlen(\+Sys\+Drive\+Device\+Path))) == 0) 3 else if (Extra\+Boot\+Partition\+Device\+Path == path) 0 else 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mount\+Volume()}{MountVolume()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int Mount\+Volume (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{H\+W\+ND}]{hwnd\+Dlg,  }\item[{int}]{drive\+No,  }\item[{char $\ast$}]{volume\+Path,  }\item[{\hyperlink{struct_password}{Password} $\ast$}]{password,  }\item[{B\+O\+OL}]{cache\+Password,  }\item[{B\+O\+OL}]{shared\+Access,  }\item[{const \hyperlink{struct_mount_options}{Mount\+Options} $\ast$const}]{mount\+Options,  }\item[{B\+O\+OL}]{quiet,  }\item[{B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Report\+Wrong\+Password }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Mount the volume safely, check if it is running well and return the value Use only cached passwords if password = N\+U\+LL. 

Returns\+: -\/1 = user aborted mount / error 0 = mount failed 1 = mount OK 2 = mount OK in shared mode

Note that some code calling this relies on the content of the mount\+Options struct to remain unmodified (don\textquotesingle{}t remove the \textquotesingle{}const\textquotesingle{} without proper revision).

\mbox{\Hypertarget{_dlgcode_8c_a6d6a25e4338d75cb5d87bcc297d1ca03}\label{_dlgcode_8c_a6d6a25e4338d75cb5d87bcc297d1ca03}} 
\index{Dlgcode.\+c@{Dlgcode.\+c}!Render\+Bitmap@{Render\+Bitmap}}
\index{Render\+Bitmap@{Render\+Bitmap}!Dlgcode.\+c@{Dlgcode.\+c}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Render\+Bitmap()}{RenderBitmap()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily H\+B\+I\+T\+M\+AP Render\+Bitmap (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char $\ast$}]{resource,  }\item[{H\+W\+ND}]{hwnd\+Dest,  }\item[{int}]{x,  }\item[{int}]{y,  }\item[{int}]{n\+Width,  }\item[{int}]{n\+Height,  }\item[{B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Direct\+Render,  }\item[{B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Keep\+Aspect\+Ratio }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Renders the specified bitmap at the specified location and stretches it to fit (anti-\/aliasing is applied). If b\+Direct\+Render is F\+A\+L\+SE and both n\+Width and n\+Height are zero, the width and height of hwnd\+Dest are retrieved and adjusted according to screen D\+PI (the width and height of the resultant image are adjusted the same way); furthermore, if b\+Keep\+Aspect\+Ratio is T\+R\+UE, the smaller D\+PI factor of the two (i.\+e. horiz. or vert.) is used both for horiz. and vert. scaling (note that the overall G\+UI aspect ratio changes irregularly in both directions depending on the D\+PI). If b\+Direct\+Render is T\+R\+UE, b\+Keep\+Aspect\+Ratio is ignored. This function returns a handle to the scaled bitmap. When the bitmap is no longer needed, it should be deleted by calling Delete\+Object() with the handle passed as the parameter. Known Windows issues\+: 


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item For some reason, anti-\/aliasing is not applied if the source bitmap contains less than 16K pixels.
\item Windows 2000 may produce slightly inaccurate colors even when source, buffer, and target are 24-\/bit true color. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em B\+O\+OL} & b\+Keep\+Aspect\+Ratio \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em B\+O\+OL} & b\+Direct\+Render \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em int} & n\+Height \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em int} & n\+Width \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em int} & y \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em int} & x \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em H\+W\+ND} & hwnd\+Dest \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em char} & $\ast$ resource \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
H\+B\+I\+T\+M\+AP hbmp\+Rescaled 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyItemize}Here is the call graph for this function\+:

{\footnotesize\ttfamily B\+O\+OL Save\+Buffer\+To\+File (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{input\+Buffer,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{destination\+File,  }\item[{D\+W\+O\+RD}]{input\+Length,  }\item[{B\+O\+OL}]{b\+Append }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



If b\+Append is T\+R\+UE, the buffer is appended to an existing file. If b\+Append is F\+A\+L\+SE, any existing file is replaced. If an error occurs, the incomplete file is deleted (provided that b\+Append is F\+A\+L\+SE) and the function returns false.
